## Idea

The sign of a permutation is defined as the parity of the length of the decomposition of the permutation into transpositions. We show that each such decomposition as the same parity, so the sign map is well defined. We then show that the sign map is a group homomorphism.

## Definitions

### The sign homomorphism into ℤ/2

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6038" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6045" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6045" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6049" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6050" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6050" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6052" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6054" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6059" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6061" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6062" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6062" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6064" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6066" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="6067" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6069" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6070" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6072" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6074" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4969" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6087" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6050" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="6089" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6062" class="Bound">n</a><a id="6090" class="Symbol">)</a> 
  <a id="6095" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="6104" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6104" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6130" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6132" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1210" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="6136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6137" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5064" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6155" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6156" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6160" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="6164" class="Number">2</a>
  <a id="6168" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6104" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6194" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6194" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6196" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6202" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="6206" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6207" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#1018" class="Function">center</a> <a id="6214" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6215" href="finite-group-theory.permutations.html#20655" class="Function">is-contr-parity-transposition-permutation</a> <a id="6257" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6062" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6259" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6261" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6194" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6262" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="6268" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6268" class="Function">preserves-add-sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6308" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6314" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6315" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6315" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6317" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6317" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6321" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6322" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5064" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6340" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6341" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6343" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="6345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6346" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5064" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6364" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6365" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6368" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="6545" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#5581" class="Function">apply-universal-property-trunc-Prop</a>
      <a id="6587" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6589" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5170" class="Function">has-cardinality-type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6623" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6624" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="6632" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6634" href="foundation-core.sets.html#1407" class="Function">Id-Prop</a>

        <a id="6671" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6673" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6104" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6700" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6535" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6702" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7855" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="6705" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6537" class="Bound">g</a><a id="6706" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="6717" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6719" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6155" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="6727" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6728" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6104" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6754" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6535" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6755" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6757" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6758" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6104" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6784" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6537" class="Bound">g</a><a id="6785" class="Symbol">)))</a>
      <a id="6795" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6797" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6799" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6799" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6801" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="6811" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6813" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2853" class="Function">ap</a>

      <a id="9387" href="univalent-combinatorics.lists.html#2156" class="Datatype">list</a>

            <a id="9458" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9460" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="9462" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9462" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9464" class="Symbol">→</a>
              <a id="9480" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4792" class="Function">has-cardinality</a> <a id="9496" class="Number">2</a>
                <a id="9514" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9516" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#502" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="9518" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9519" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5064" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="9537" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6070" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9538" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9540" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9543" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9543" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9545" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9547" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2141" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="9567" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9568" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9462" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9570" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9543" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9571" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
    <a id="9581" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9265" class="Function">list-trans</a> <a id="9592" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9592" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="9595" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9595" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="9597" class="Symbol">=</a>

### Deloopings of the sign homomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="11793" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="11800" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#11800" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="11804" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="11806" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#11806" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="11808" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11810" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="11815" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="11819" class="Keyword">where</a>
  
  <a id="11830" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#11830" class="Function">map-cartier-delooping-sign</a> <a id="11857" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11859" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11860" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#11860" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="11862" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11864" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1444" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11865" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11867" class="Symbol">→</a>

### Simpson's delooping of the sign homomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="22250" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="22257" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#22257" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="29302" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="29304" href="foundation.equivalence-classes.html#3224" class="Function">type-class-large-set-quotient</a>
